              // Initialize image error handler immediately
              (function() {
                const failedImages = new Set();
                window.addEventListener('error', function(event) {
                  const target = event.target;
                  if (target.tagName === 'IMG') {
                    event.preventDefault();
                    const src = target.src;
                    if (!failedImages.has(src) && !src.includes('/no-image.svg')) {
                      failedImages.add(src);
                      // target.src = '/no-image.svg'; // Removed to prevent hydration mismatch. React components handle their own fallbacks.
                      // target.alt = 'Image not available'; // Removed to prevent hydration mismatch
                      console.warn('⚠️ Image failed:', src);
                    }
                  }
                  if (target.tagName === 'LINK') {
                    event.preventDefault();
                    console.warn('⚠️ Icon failed:', target.href);
                  }
                }, true);
                
                window.addEventListener('unhandledrejection', function(event) {
                  console.error('❌ Unhandled error:', event.reason);
                  event.preventDefault();
                });
              })();
